ain,p]::1;[https://nautil.us/pursuing-covid-19-at-internet-speed-11453,p]::1;[https://www.nationalgeographic.com/magazine/article/why-are-people-so-dang-obsessed-with-mars-feature,p]::1;[https://nautil.us/ebook,p]::2;[https://medlineplus.gov/genetics/understanding/mutationsanddisorders/genemutation,p]::1;[https://www.chromeexperiments.com,t]::2;[https://www.chromeexperiments.com,h]::2;[https://www.chromeexperiments.com,p]::4;[https://www.englishclub.com/vocabulary/vaccine.php,p]::1;[https://www.nytimes.com/interactive/2022/03/18/technology/cryptocurrency-crypto-guide.html,p]::1;[https://www.englishclub.com/vocabulary/censorship.php,p]::1;[https://icons8.com/our-business-model,p]::1;[https://www.sciencenews.org,h]::2;[https://www.sciencenewsforstudents.org/collections/experiments,t]::1;[https://www.sciencenewsforstudents.org/collections/experiments,h]::1;[https://www.sciencenewsforstudents.org/collections,h]::1;[https://www.sciencenewsforstudents.org/collections/experiments,p]::1;[https://www.dailymail.co.uk/sciencetech/index.html,h]::1;[https://www.dailymail.co.uk/sciencetech/index.html,p]::1;[https://www.sciencenewsforstudents.org/how-to-use,p]::3;
